  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e6f6d040-f066-416c-8aa8-1beb150a9a0e'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer12232062534699167930">Sara Grey’s world shattered ten years ago when her father was brutally murdered. Now at seventeen, she is still haunted by memories of that day and driven by the need to understand why it happened. She lives a life full of secrets and her family and friends have no idea of the supernatural world she is immersed in or of Sara’s own very powerful gift.<br/><br/>In her quest for answer</span>
  <span id="freeText12232062534699167930" style="display:none">Sara Grey’s world shattered ten years ago when her father was brutally murdered. Now at seventeen, she is still haunted by memories of that day and driven by the need to understand why it happened. She lives a life full of secrets and her family and friends have no idea of the supernatural world she is immersed in or of Sara’s own very powerful gift.<br /><br />In her quest for answers about her father’s death, Sara takes risks that expose her and her friends to danger and puts herself into the sights of a sadistic vampire. On the same fateful night she meets Nikolas, a warrior who turns Sara’s world upside down and is determined to protect her even if it’s the last thing she wants.<br /><br />Sara’s life starts to spin out of control as she is hunted by an obsessed vampire, learns that her friends have secrets of their own and reels from the truth about her own ancestry. Sara has always been fiercely independent but in order to survive now she must open herself to others, to reveal her deepest secrets. And she must learn to trust the one person capable of breaking down the walls around her.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Yes. When I skimmed the reviews it made it seem like there wasn't any. It's urban fantasy rather than a paranormal romance...like there isn't heavy on<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Yes. When I skimmed the reviews it made it seem like there wasn't any. It's urban fantasy rather than a paranormal romance...like there isn't heavy on the romance part yet (not the focus of the book), but there is a love interest . similar to Vampire Academy #1<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

  <i>*****AUGUST 26: THIS IS FREE FOR KINDLE. IF YOU HAVEN'T CHECKED IT OUT YET, WHATS WRONG WITH YOU!?***** </i>
</b><br />-------&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.com/B00HJ9N3JU">http://amzn.com/B00HJ9N3JU</a><br /><br /><b>MAY 2015:</b> <i>Apparently I need to just...reread all my favorite books from this year.....*sigh*</i><br /><br />I haven't really stopped thinking about this book since I finished it the first time around back in January. It starts out kind of slow, there really isn't anything special about it....but then you read on, and you start to piece together what Sara is all about. <br /><br />This book is a lovely mix of <b>vampire, werewolf, troll and faerie</b> stories, along with some other creatures. <i>You would think, that it would be just a mess with so many supernatural creatures, but it really does work here.</i><br /><br />I said it before, and I will repeat that it is <b>beautifully written</b>. I love it as much as I did the first time around, maybe even more...Sara wasn't as much of a pain as I originally thought. I love all the characters here, <i>Lynch definitely did it right when she introduced us to each of them.</i> <b>Also, you can't beat Nikolas Danshov.</b> He is my top fictional boyfriend. I love him! He is the best. <br /><br /><i><b>I recommend this to everyone</b>, really...its so good! definitely one of the top favorite books [series...] I've ever read.</i><br /><br />------------<br /><br /><b>JAN 2015</b> <s>I hate finishing such amazing books. this one was beautifully written. there were times I wasn't so fond of the main character...but she's pretty bad ass all in all. I am looking forward to getting my hands on the next one!</s></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564736281" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8279200496067951839">Downloaded for free from Amazon.co.uk<br/><br/>This was a YA fantasy story about a girl who could heal. <br/><br/>Sara was an okay character, but she did seem to put herself at risk a lot. I got that she cared for both people and animals when they were suffering, but she could have been more careful, especially when it came to meeting strangers, and she seemed to spill her secrets to more and more people as the book went on.<br/><br/>The storyline in this was about Sara learning that she wasn’t fully human, and learning that</span>
  <span id="freeText8279200496067951839" style="display:none">Downloaded for free from Amazon.co.uk<br><br>This was a YA fantasy story about a girl who could heal. <br><br>Sara was an okay character, but she did seem to put herself at risk a lot. I got that she cared for both people and animals when they were suffering, but she could have been more careful, especially when it came to meeting strangers, and she seemed to spill her secrets to more and more people as the book went on.<br><br>The storyline in this was about Sara learning that she wasn’t fully human, and learning that people were searching for her because of it. Why the news about her not being human was a surprise though, I don’t know. It’s not like normal humans go around healing animals with their bare hands. I felt like the story took a long while to get going though, and it never fully held my attention.<br><br>The ending to this was okay, although it was obvious that the story would continue in the next book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433066531i/15045433.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6 out of 10</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33416536-eroticaafterdark-lilith?shelf=non-erotica">non-erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1247423248" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1382439937479400860"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440417841ra/15973105.gif' alt='disappointment' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh my... this book.... had too much of everything...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432623301ra/14990151.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Stupidity, plot-holes, mystical creatures, alleged plot-twists, people, more stupidity, mood swings, but hey! at least no kissing!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/264612.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432624802ra/14990410.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>... okay, that's not positive.<br/><br/>But let's start with the good things first: the Mohiri. I won't forestall what those are, but the idea - even though how they came to being isn't logical for me - was pretty good.<br/>All the mythical creature overload, sylphs (air elementals), trolls, vampires (actually demons), werewolfs</span>
  <span id="freeText1382439937479400860" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440417841ra/15973105.gif" alt="disappointment" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh my... this book.... had too much of everything...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432623301ra/14990151.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Stupidity, plot-holes, mystical creatures, alleged plot-twists, people, more stupidity, mood swings, but hey! at least no kissing!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/264612.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432624802ra/14990410.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>... okay, that's not positive.<br><br>But let's start with the good things first: the Mohiri. I won't forestall what those are, but the idea - even though how they came to being isn't logical for me - was pretty good.<br>All the mythical creature overload, sylphs (air elementals), trolls, vampires (actually demons), werewolfs, demon-hunters (actually demons, too), male witches (that was awesome). The only overload I though was pretty cool.<br>The writing is good, it was an easy read, though my eyes still hurt from rolling. But we're still with the good things, right? Right.<br><br>Sadly, there isn't much for me. I liked the friendships, even though the final explanation ruined it a little.... honestly the final explanation about why and how and what the BIG CAPITAL F is Sara ruined pretty much everything. It annoys me so much, I cannot even write a structured review.<br><br>I liked that there wasn't really romance and the boy, who obviously fancied Sarah and whom she liked to, had nothing to do with the whole story, which was nice. And he respected her wishes, which was nice. What wasn't nice that even this got ruined through the final revelation about Sara.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432624772ra/14990406.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sara pretty much ruined everything about this story. I don't mind a naïve character, but I expect character development from the MAIN female character. But there was close to NONE. Which is why I cannot recommend this book to anyone.<br>Yes, the need of helping others is not a bad thing and a really good character trait as long as you THINK before you act. It doesn't help if you want to protect and help people, when you but them in MORE danger through your actions.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432624772ra/14990407.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me not start about the plotholes.... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Troll bile can cure even cancer and apparently Alzheimers, but dear Sara doesn't give it a try on her paralyzed uncle??????? She gets attacked and taken hostage by a vampire but her 'beast' that stirs almost every time does not burst into action? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I won't talk about the twilight chemistry, or the true blood faerie land...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432624772ra/14990408.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sorry, but I cannot cheer for a female character that does everything wrong and is still the hero. Plus her being <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[a Mohiri and a undine? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432624772ra/14990409.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>sorry, no sorry. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>This character ruined the book for me.<br><br>No, I won't continue the series. 1.5 rounded to 2, because I definitely wasn't part of the target market.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440429210ra/15974231.gif" alt="1.5 stars" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440417551ra/15973092.gif" alt="disclaimer" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12711974173410167462"><b>Read #2</b><br/>Buddy read with, Louise! I link her review once it's up.<br/><br/>This book is great! It's obviously not as good as the rest of them (because let's face it, the others are AH-MAZING) because it's primarily set-up of the supernatural world. There is plenty of action, but it's only the beginning. <br/><br/>I needed some romance (which is why I'm also rereading book two; I need some Nikolas deliciousness) but I really respect and appreciate the fact that there isn't any romance in this book.<br/>I like this move by </span>
  <span id="freeText12711974173410167462" style="display:none"><b>Read #2</b><br>Buddy read with, Louise! I link her review once it's up.<br><br>This book is great! It's obviously not as good as the rest of them (because let's face it, the others are AH-MAZING) because it's primarily set-up of the supernatural world. There is plenty of action, but it's only the beginning. <br><br>I needed some romance (which is why I'm also rereading book two; I need some Nikolas deliciousness) but I really respect and appreciate the fact that there isn't any romance in this book.<br>I like this move by Karen because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sara and Nikolas are mates <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and the lack of romantic interaction in the entirety of the first book solidifies the relationship as one not based on an immediate attraction!<br><br>So I reread this book in French because I'm studying French and would really like to improve.<br><br>It was hard.<br>And it was the first full-length novel I've read in French. I started reading it back in October and didn't finish it until the end of January because a) I had the most insane semester ever and b) it was hard.<br>There were a LOT of words I did not know and I couldn't exactly go and look them all up because I would have been an old woman by the time I finished.<br>I realized that the less I focused on each individual word, the more I understood due to increased flow. With any text, you can't just read the words; you have to take a step back and look at the big picture. Often, because this was in a different language, I forgot to take a step back because I panicked. <br>But I did take a step back and found that I was reading faster and understanding more. I was definitely a rough journey, but I'm excited to do it again! I learned so many new and useful vocabulary words that I can apply and I'm so happy!!<br><br><u>
  <b>To any of you studying a foreign language: I recommend finding a book that you have already read and adored in the language you're studying. It's an incredibly useful step in the process!</b>
</u><br><br><br>_______________________________________<br><b>Read #1&gt;<br><br>I should have written a review for this a long time ago.<br>Now, what I remember is very limited.<br>I just remember that it was pretty darn awesome!<br><br>Honestly, I was confused as to why everyone crushed on Sara at some point or another.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2702163756" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2702163756" />
    <a title="Lena K." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46184829-lena-k"><img alt="Lena K." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559055379p2/46184829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2702163756?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lena K." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lena K." href="/user/show/46184829-lena-k">Lena K.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/25495480-relentless">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46184829-lena-k?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46184829-lena-k?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2702163756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5863355635018587875"><b>
  <i>“Sometimes I thought of us as a pair of damaged bookends. We both had our flaws but we belonged together even if there was always something between us, keeping us apart.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Book-related quotes always buy me over. So there’s that.<br/><br/>The cover is…uhm not my cup of tea. I like to imagine the characters myself, and the half faces ruined that for me, and now they’re stuck in my head! <br/><br/>Sarah lives with her uncle and heals animals, imps and other magical beings called ‘The People’. One night she goes to a</span>
  <span id="freeText5863355635018587875" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“Sometimes I thought of us as a pair of damaged bookends. We both had our flaws but we belonged together even if there was always something between us, keeping us apart.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Book-related quotes always buy me over. So there’s that.<br /><br />The cover is…uhm not my cup of tea. I like to imagine the characters myself, and the half faces ruined that for me, and now they’re stuck in my head! <br /><br />Sarah lives with her uncle and heals animals, imps and other magical beings called ‘The People’. One night she goes to a party and meets a vampire. Everything goes wrong from there. Stay tuned! <br /><br />Sarah is a special snowflake, A VERY SPECIAL SNOWFLAKE, as it will turn out. And she acts like it. I mean, yeah, she’s kind and compassionate and heals animals, tries to help everyone (and gets in a mess, because that’s what happens when you don’t think before you act) while being a good friend and a human being, which is great. BUT, like I said, she’s a special snowflake; every boy/werewolf/vampire/mohiri is attracted to her, every girl hates her and is insanely jealous of her. She likes classic rock music and knows who Janis Joplin is, while the other girls squeak and squeal and love Backstreetboys… She’s also, obviously, a tom boy and totally not aware of the boys’ attention. I’m sorry but this is getting old, this hatred and aversion from ‘girly’ traits. The explanation in the end as to WHY all the boys like her and all the girls hate her, doesn’t completely absolve this trait, since like I mentioned, in her eyes, the other girls only think about hot boys (while Sarah is of course, totally oblivious of them and of her affect on them) and act nasty towards her because of it. <br /><br />I did like the fact that even though she has a Mohiri (half-demon vampire hunters) bad-ass bodyguards, two werewolf friends and a best friend in the form of a troll, she can stand for herself, and doesn’t (well…usefully that is) need saving. You go, snowflake! <br /><br />The writing was nice and flawing, and the plot was ok, that is, except for the plot holes… For example; her healing doesn’t work on humans so she can’t heal her wheel-chaired uncle. BUT, there is a potent spoilery thingy that can cure even cancer and Alzheimer’s and prolong life. WHY in the name of all the faeries didn’t Sarah try it on her uncle?! Second major plot hole was in the end, when Sarah got in trouble (again…) and the bad-ass mohiri bodyguard (that I definitely don’t have a crush on) gets to the right place at the right time, even though no one except Sarah and her troll friend knew about that place. How very convenient… <br /><br />All in all it was a nice read and I’ll continue to the second book in the hopes that it will get better and will have more Nikolas screen time :P</span>
  <a data-text-id="5863355635018587875" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_829651180" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/829651180" />
    <a title="David Blanton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27886119-david-blanton"><img alt="David Blanton" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/829651180?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="David Blanton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="David Blanton" href="/user/show/27886119-david-blanton">David Blanton</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer829651180" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5297578104054422080">I usually don't get into this genre, but it looked interesting so I decided to give it a go. Once I got started I was floored by the author's style. The characters are all believable and they are developed in such a way that you don't have to spend time with 4 or 5 chapters of filler before the action begins. She gets into it right away and develops the characters as you get into the flow of the book. It is kind of reminiscent of the way one of favorite authors Terry Brooks does it in his Word a</span>
  <span id="freeText5297578104054422080" style="display:none">I usually don't get into this genre, but it looked interesting so I decided to give it a go. Once I got started I was floored by the author's style. The characters are all believable and they are developed in such a way that you don't have to spend time with 4 or 5 chapters of filler before the action begins. She gets into it right away and develops the characters as you get into the flow of the book. It is kind of reminiscent of the way one of favorite authors Terry Brooks does it in his Word and the Void series. I found myself starting to try to figure out how these crazy characters were going to interact and trying to get the plot before it happened. A good author gives you a little bit but then throws a twist at you that you wouldn't expect and the author delivers in spades with this book. While the characters had definitive good and evil structure to them they also showed a respect for each others abilities, well except for the ugly toothsome baddies. In the end I was left looking for more, not because of a lack of content, but because of I had grown to care what happened to these characters. I am patiently awaiting the 2nd and 3rd novel in this trilogy! Great job and I would recommend this book to anyone who likes to read about the struggle between good and evil and is looking for a couple of days of escape from the rat race we live in. If you take more than a couple of days to read this book you ain't doin' it right!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5297578104054422080" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3127130851" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3127130851" />
    <a title="Bookadmirer " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/103293496-bookadmirer"><img alt="Bookadmirer " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601720853p2/103293496.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3127130851?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookadmirer " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookadmirer " href="/user/show/103293496-bookadmirer">Bookadmirer </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3127130851" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18090906390196985669">I loved this book. It was adventurous and the plot is great. There are so many creatures in this book. It's confusing and entertaining at the same time but the latter part was more prominent because I enjoyed it. There isn't any romance in this book, I hope it changes in the next book because I absolutely love Nicholas and Sara together. One thing I didn't like is, it's a very lengthy book. I felt the author could have shortened it.</span>

  <span id="freeText13335873213675094751" style="display:none">I recently discovered Karen Lynch and her amazing debut novel Relentless. I read almost constantly in the YA Paranormal/fantasy genre and it is so difficult finding something different, enticing and very well written. But here it is.<br /><br />From the first pages with Remy (I LOVE HIM) I was sucked in. I really liked Sara, I loved the relationship she has with her 'brothers' and the romance aspect felt perfect. Not insta-love, but the bones of what feels like could be an epic love-story. And the way all the supernatural creatures merged together seamlessly was very well done. The creatures aren't new but the story feels original. <br /><br />The story wraps up nicely, leaving just enough intrigue that I'll be waiting to read the next chapter for sure. </span>

  <span id="freeText10601178483120910625" style="display:none">3.5 out of 5 Stars...I think...<br /><br />If I'm being honest, I'm not sure how this book found its way into my hands. Not only physically (for real I have no recollection of purchasing this), but also what lured me into starting this yesterday afternoon. <br /><br />And Lord was I ill prepared for what I signed up for. First of all, I had no clue this was book 1 in a 6-deep series...so far...?... Second, I wasn't expecting how chock-full of creatures this book was going to be. Seriously you name it and it was in there: Vampires, werewolves, fae, elementals, vampire hunters, gobels, trolls, hybrids, offensive stereotyped villains, etc. <br /><br /><b>And ALL in 280 pages!!!</b><br /><br />I want to read more since I suspect book 1 was basically foundation for the journey ahead, but I'm also fearful of what might be around the bend if so much made its way into book 1!<br /><br />If I'm being totally honest a MAJOR factor in my decision to read book 2 is to get me some more Nikolai.<br /><br />What <i>IS</i> it with fictional characters named Nikolai?!?!?<br /><br />Full RTC once I've sorted my thoughts. Has anyone else read this? I need to discuss asap!</span>

<div id="review_841146291" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/841146291" />
    <a title="Mary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7593236-mary"><img alt="Mary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459025664p2/7593236.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/841146291?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary" href="/user/show/7593236-mary">Mary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Urban Fantasy lovers, YA lovers, and anyone who is looking for a seriously good read</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Mary by: </span>
      Karen Lynch
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer841146291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6023811628277065124">ALRIGHT!<br/><br/>Let me start off by saying that I went into this book practically drooling. By the time I actually sat down to read it, I had seen the cover multiple times, read various samples, and even heard my friend talk about what was going on in the story. So I was EXCITED FOR THIS BOOK.<br/><br/>And it did not disappoint! When I started thinking about what to mention in my review, one item in particular stuck out: Gender.<br/><br/>I am so unbelievably PROUD of Karen for making a character who can be friends with a b</span>
  <span id="freeText6023811628277065124" style="display:none">ALRIGHT!<br /><br />Let me start off by saying that I went into this book practically drooling. By the time I actually sat down to read it, I had seen the cover multiple times, read various samples, and even heard my friend talk about what was going on in the story. So I was EXCITED FOR THIS BOOK.<br /><br />And it did not disappoint! When I started thinking about what to mention in my review, one item in particular stuck out: Gender.<br /><br />I am so unbelievably PROUD of Karen for making a character who can be friends with a bunch of guys WITHOUT any romantic notions on either side (okay sure Peter and Roland both had crushes on Sara but that went away pretty quickly and they were still friends afterwards). As a seventeen year old girl who has had to put up with being friends with a guy and then being subsequently told "OHMYGAWD you guys would be SO cute together!" by dozens of other people, I am glad that Karen addressed the fact that friendship does not mean romantic interest. THANK YOU KAREN I LOVE YOU.<br /><br />If there's any one thing that could possibly put people off from this book, it's the typos. As with any published work, things go unnoticed. Sometimes a letter would be switched out with another (which a lot of word processors do!! grrr) or a word would be added ("Remy's has" happened once :P), but they were all excusable errors and did not distract me for too long from the plot (not to mention the fact that the plot was GLORIOUS). <br /><br />ALL IN ALL I LIKE THIS BOOK A LOT. Like a lot a lot. And it is TOTALLY worth reading! I finished it in the middle of the school day and immediately passed it on to one of my best friends and commanded her to start reading it right that instant. It's so good that I want to share it with people and any book that can make a person want to share it is a fabulous book indeed. So Karen did a WONDERFUL MARVELOUS SPECTACULAR STUPENDOUS JOB and I will be on the look out for the sequel!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! (and, you know, the last book in the trilogy, too)</span>
  <a data-text-id="6023811628277065124" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5099441988540685079" style="display:none">Okay, first of I'm an honest reviewer and if the book is bad, I'll say so. Now lemme proceed. <br /><br />This book is a <b> 4.98 stars </b> book<br /><br />The book begins a bit too slowly for my liking, and the beginning of the book definitely did not capture my attention. The actual story started when a bit later when the mc was introduced, and from then I could not put the book down. <br /><br />The development of the plot is beautiful, every twist and turn leaves you breathless, and I was honestly clawing my heart out in the sudden twist of plot, and that my people is the beauty of this book. <br /><br />Now coming to the character development<br /><br />Sara Grey: I personally liked the character because she wasn't stupid and she understood what was going on around her, and in utter honesty she didn't need anyone to protect her because she didn't want anyone to risk their life for hers. Her character potrays a strong and independent female lead whom I admire.<br /><br />Nikolas Danshov: In honesty is it just me or Nikolas totally resembles Derek Hale from Teen Wolf? His utter intelligence and his rage are my most favorite bits of him. He is worth drooling over, although there is not much of a review of him in this book, I'm telling you, the next book you'll literally rip your heart out.<br /><br />That being said <b>
  <i> HOW IS THIS BOOK NAHT FAMOUS LIKE SERIOUSLY? DO YOU GUYS KNOW HOW HARD IT IS TO GET MY HANDS ON SUCH GOOD BOOKS? LIKE WHY DON'T PEOPLE READ BOOKS THAT ARE ACTUALLY SO FUCKEN GOOD LIKE WHAT! </b>  phew a fangirl moment up there but seriously. This book is dope.<br /><br />READ THIS BOOK no matter what because trust me its got a 5 star from me, a person who normally keeps away from supernatural stuff but this book.............. phew seriously.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1205444279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17914370198156658259">You know you've just read an amazing book when all you have to criticize is the lack of a few commas. It makes me sad to think about how close I'd come to not reading this little gem at all, as I wasn't too fond of the UF genre as a whole at the time I stumbled across it, and it being a Freebie on Amazon when my experinces with those weren't the best... well, let's just say I was suspicious at the least.<br/><br/>However, Karen Lynch did everything right with this novel. Fantastic, well-developed main and</span>
  <span id="freeText17914370198156658259" style="display:none">You know you've just read an amazing book when all you have to criticize is the lack of a few commas. It makes me sad to think about how close I'd come to not reading this little gem at all, as I wasn't too fond of the UF genre as a whole at the time I stumbled across it, and it being a Freebie on Amazon when my experinces with those weren't the best... well, let's just say I was suspicious at the least.<br><br>However, Karen Lynch did everything right with this novel. Fantastic, well-developed main and secondary characters. An elaborate and suspenseful plot. Intriguing world building. A perfect mix of funny banter, gripping action and mind-boggling fantasy elements.<br><br>Let's start with the characters. <br>Sara was the perfect female lead. Independent and strong, yet kind-hearted and endowed with a super power of unknown origin. She doesn't take crap from anyone and though she is stubborn, she knows when it's time to step back and let someone more suitable take over. Speaking of...<br>I have the biggest crush on Nikolas. He is one of those infamous silent, brooding, overbearing heroes but, unlike so many others with those traits, he's not being a jerk about it. He's protective and a fierce and loyal warrior, and, I'll just call it as it is, totally hot.<br>Nate, even though he's just Sara's uncle, must be one of the best father figures I've come across in the YA genre so far, with his patience and sympathy for Sara, without being neglectful of his duties as a 'parent'. Go Nate!<br>Then there are all the secondary characters... Roland, Peter, Chris, and even Samson. All of them lovable in their own way and a great addition to this story.<br>And let's not forget about Eli, the villain. I loved him, too, in a very twisted kind of way.<br><br>As for the storyline, there wasn't a single page in this book that made me wish for more. I virtually devoured it in one session, pausing only when absolutely necessary. There were unforeseeable twists and turns of events, unexpected revelations, action and a budding romance <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that won't lead to anything until the sequel, though <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. We're being introduced to a variety of fantastical creatures - demons, trolls, fae, werewolves and many more. And know what's best? This book doesn't glorify vampires. Yay!<br><br>This is one of those books I wish I could forget all about - only to be able to read it again and again without knowing what's going to happen. Not that it matters. I'll read it again and again anyway.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444295338ra/16481860.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oooooh yes, I did. I really did. I added a One Direction GIF to my review. If I succumb to fangirling, I might aswell do it right!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1443097360" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1443097360" />
    <a title="Maggie ☘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40477684-maggie"><img alt="Maggie ☘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591529603p2/40477684.jpg" /></a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1443097360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8069385924302058682"><b>*2.5 - not my cup of tea - stars*</b><br/><br/>I was hoping for something like this- <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13482750.Sanctum__Guards_of_the_Shadowlands___1_' title='Sanctum (Guards of the Shadowlands, #1) by Sarah Fine' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sanctum</a> or this- <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_' title='Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A.E. Kirk' rel='nofollow noopener'>Demons at Deadnight</a>. <br/><br/>Unfortunately, what I've got was another mix between Vampire Academy (which I LOVE btw! But this was just trying to copy way too har at times, especially with the love interest) and Twilight. <i>Relentless </i> definitely wasn't a bad book, but it sure wasn't anything remarkable either. Just a perfectly normal (band) paranormal book.<br/><br/>One of the better things about this book was definitely the mix</span>
  <span id="freeText8069385924302058682" style="display:none"><b>*2.5 - not my cup of tea - stars*</b><br /><br />I was hoping for something like this- <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13482750.Sanctum__Guards_of_the_Shadowlands___1_" title="Sanctum (Guards of the Shadowlands, #1) by Sarah Fine" rel="nofollow noopener">Sanctum</a> or this- <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16067683.Demons_at_Deadnight__Divinicus_Nex_Chronicles___1_" title="Demons at Deadnight (Divinicus Nex Chronicles, #1) by A.E. Kirk" rel="nofollow noopener">Demons at Deadnight</a>. <br /><br />Unfortunately, what I've got was another mix between Vampire Academy (which I LOVE btw! But this was just trying to copy way too har at times, especially with the love interest) and Twilight. <i>Relentless </i> definitely wasn't a bad book, but it sure wasn't anything remarkable either. Just a perfectly normal (band) paranormal book.<br /><br />One of the better things about this book was definitely the mix of different paranormal creatures - trolls, goblins, vampires, werewolves, fae and witches. <br /><br />Sara - she's kind, stubborn and would do anything for her uncle and friends. I think that she has the potencial to become really interesting heroine in the next book. Update: Which she does in book three! Like she would never be among my all time favorite characters or anything, but I fucking admired her in the last instalment! Also, the series does get better as it goes on, this is definitely the blandest book of them all so I wouldn't exactly not recommend it 'cause I actually did enjoy reading book three.<br /><br /><b>“If I ever got this stupid over a guy I hoped someone would slap some sense into me.” </b><br /><br />Nikolas- if you're into mysterious he-man warriors, I guess you'll like him. But I personally wasn't taken with him so much. He was a bit balnd to me. <br /><br />Apart from the interesting creatures, <i>Relentless</i> reminds me of too many other paranormal books I have read so far. The characters weren't annoying but I wasn't really taken with them either and the storyline was a bit simple and predictable. But if you haven't read too many paranormal books and want something entertaining and fast-paced, than try <i>Relentless</i>. <br /><br /><b>“When you keep to yourself, people will fill in the details about your life themselves.”</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8069385924302058682" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Yes it was the good. <br/><br/>I love urban fantasy and I went google searching for books that have hate-to-love type relationships because those are my favorite and I came across a slew of books with that troupe that I hadn't read and this trilogy was one of them. <br/><br/>Sara has always known that she was different, she's always known that there was another world out there, one with all the mythical creatures you can imagine, from thieving imps, t</span>
  <span id="freeText8475379699772695928" style="display:none">Well this was an unexpected delight that I read within 24 hours. Yes it was the good. <br /><br />I love urban fantasy and I went google searching for books that have hate-to-love type relationships because those are my favorite and I came across a slew of books with that troupe that I hadn't read and this trilogy was one of them. <br /><br />Sara has always known that she was different, she's always known that there was another world out there, one with all the mythical creatures you can imagine, from thieving imps, to vampires and werewolves to trolls. Her world was turned upside down her father is found murdered and she knows it was a vampire that did it. <br />Then came the fact that she has powers to heal, and befriends a troll and together they help heal other mythical creatures while her troll friend Remy teaches her about this other world they actually live in.<br /><br />Then one night Sara is almost eaten by a vampire and she then is introduced to a secret warrior society call Moirir that you are born into but she never knew about. She is asked to join to which she refuses and the guy named Nikolas who not only saved her life but is now trying to get her to leave the only life she has ever known and loves. <br /><br />Nikolas and Sara don't get along and she defies him every step of the way and I loved it. She is still a girl but also a stubborn, strong willed character and I love Sara. <br />I love Nikolas because he isn't a jerk but is bossy which makes the dynamics between him and Sara what I love to read.<br /><br />I loved the world building and really just enjoyed the overall story. <br /><br />Sexual Content: mild<br />Language: heavy<br />Drugs/Alcohol: moderate<br />Violence: heavy</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=satans-brother-steve">satans-brother-steve</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860117132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3401831948180651773"> <b>Special fried rice.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442433569i/16233791.jpg' width='304' height='228' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You know that in any Chinese restaurant they have that one dish that is ridiculously loaded with everything that they have. You got your pork, beef, chicken, prawn and everything in between all on one plate. It makes your stomach queasy just thinking about it. Special is one word to call it. Too much is another.<br/><br/>Relentless is too much when it comes to world building. It started more than ok. It's about a girl that has healing powers and deals with the People – the Fey. But soo</span>
  <span id="freeText3401831948180651773" style="display:none"> <b>Special fried rice.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442433569i/16233791.jpg" width="304" height="228" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know that in any Chinese restaurant they have that one dish that is ridiculously loaded with everything that they have. You got your pork, beef, chicken, prawn and everything in between all on one plate. It makes your stomach queasy just thinking about it. Special is one word to call it. Too much is another.<br><br>Relentless is too much when it comes to world building. It started more than ok. It's about a girl that has healing powers and deals with the People – the Fey. But soon enough there were many different types of supernatural creatures kicking about. There were many fey represented, then we have vampires, werewolves and vampire hunters. After all that was introduced we got to know that the vampires are actually demons.<br><br>There were far too many paranormal aspects tossed in together without much care where they landed. We have vampires, werewolves and vampire hunters as a batch that is commonly found together. We have the fey and their many castes that are usually defined by elemental magic and if anything, commonly set against or apart of vampires. Then we have demons, as in angels and demons that imply religious beliefs and all that jazz that comes from mysticism from modern religions and Greek and Roman influences throughout time. <br><br>Less is more. I would have appreciated the novel more if the author took her time to delay all the introductions to all her supernatural supporting cast. In this way I didn't get a feeling that they are magical at all, in fact I got a feeling like they are a dime a dozen there. They seemed to pop up like mushrooms after rain. Without the necessary build-up and true background of every species I didn't enjoy it as I expected it to.<br><br>The second thing and the most annoying one is the Twilightish feel of the whole werewolf clan. The running away to spend some time with his cousin 'hunting' and not including her. The fact that she wasn't liked or supported when she came over, later the shock over the fact that she now knows about them, yadda yadda....yawn. I lost interest.....</span>
  <a data-text-id="3401831948180651773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1722840601" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1722840601" />
    <a title="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34403359"><img alt="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469758679p2/34403359.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1722840601?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė" href="/user/show/34403359">☆ ĄňŊǡƂėƮĦ ☆ ŞŧŎŋė</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780615942421" href="/book/show/20534422-relentless">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34403359?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1722840601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14151108039346543091"><b>5/5</b><br/><br/>Even in the beginning of this book, I knew that I was going to be hooked on it and the rest of the series. I immediately loved Sara and basically everything about this book.<br/><br/>I loved all of the fantasy/paranormal information and action in this action. The mix of werewolves, vampires, goblins, trolls, and faeries was <b>amazing</b> and not at all confusing. I have read other books involving either one or more of the creatures that I have mentioned above so I had some experience reading about them but t</span>
  <span id="freeText14151108039346543091" style="display:none"><b>5/5</b><br /><br />Even in the beginning of this book, I knew that I was going to be hooked on it and the rest of the series. I immediately loved Sara and basically everything about this book.<br /><br />I loved all of the fantasy/paranormal information and action in this action. The mix of werewolves, vampires, goblins, trolls, and faeries was <b>amazing</b> and not at all confusing. I have read other books involving either one or more of the creatures that I have mentioned above so I had some experience reading about them but there were some differences between them, which was <b>very enjoyable</b>.<br /><br />The characters were <b>wonderful</b>. I really loved Sara because she was pretty normal, not hyped up to be some strong girl, and did make some mistakes. Though with hindsight it was sometimes frustrating but who wouldn't have done differently than her in some cases? Another character I really liked was Nikolas (come on, who couldn't like him?). While I was reading this, I wrote an update saying that he reminded me of Dimitri from Vampire Academy and I stand by that now. They were both Russian, great warriors, and hunted bad vampires <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and had feelings for who they were helping/training (I'm not sure if that is a spoiler) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. The characters interactions were <b>fantasic</b> and I loved them. I can't wait to read the second book to see more about them.<br /><br />The suspense and action in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20427449.Relentless__Relentless___1_" title="Relentless (Relentless, #1) by Karen Lynch" rel="nofollow noopener">Relentless</a> is still there so it is carrying over into the second book with a kind of cliffhanger. I can't wait to start reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20883154.Refuge__Relentless__2_" title="Refuge (Relentless #2) by Karen Lynch" rel="nofollow noopener">Refuge</a>.<br /><br />I look forward to reading more by Lynch, who may become one of my favorite authors, and I recommend this book to anyone looking for a <b>very well written book</b>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14151108039346543091" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1556097944" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10210303889458814408">This book really took me by surprise. I listened to this book, and I really enjoyed the story. It was original, and I loved Sarah right away. It is an easy read/listen. Besides a few cuss words here or there (maybe 2 in the book), this is a great fantasy young adult series. I went immediatly to the second book. I am completely hooked on these characters and this story that I went straght to book 3 when I was finish with book 2. I really like this one and can't wait to see what happens.<br/><br/>I'm sure t</span>
  <span id="freeText10210303889458814408" style="display:none">This book really took me by surprise. I listened to this book, and I really enjoyed the story. It was original, and I loved Sarah right away. It is an easy read/listen. Besides a few cuss words here or there (maybe 2 in the book), this is a great fantasy young adult series. I went immediatly to the second book. I am completely hooked on these characters and this story that I went straght to book 3 when I was finish with book 2. I really like this one and can't wait to see what happens.<br /><br />I'm sure this was written when vampires were so popular. So I thought it would be like another Twilight, but this one is very original with so man side characters that you grow to love. </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VDTq7h7Hk+q7d24n4cacpyTXNaDvFUoc54Y5xTjDyDozTSELOsP5UwQVCBQWrIhJYSn9KtswMnG8KfKirkfrOA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('s0/iTsYlqefANPeErKZZ++VenHBvXC1jK+36om7fgQjUNimr4iHDXn9WkbdbzE0VoKBU+lt5VQ5wQjHF+FuiCg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer1942781539846299983">Karen Lynch is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author. <br/><br/>She grew up in Newfoundland, Canada - a place rich in colorful people and folklore to which she attributes her love of the supernatural and her vivid imagination. She moved to Charlotte, North Carolina years ago and was immediately charmed by the southern people but she says she will always be a newfie.<br/><br/>Though she loves supernatural </span>
  <span id="freeText1942781539846299983" style="display:none">Karen Lynch is a New York Times and USA Today bestselling author. <br /><br />She grew up in Newfoundland, Canada - a place rich in colorful people and folklore to which she attributes her love of the supernatural and her vivid imagination. She moved to Charlotte, North Carolina years ago and was immediately charmed by the southern people but she says she will always be a newfie.<br /><br />Though she loves supernatural fiction, she has a soft spot for Charlotte Brontë and Jane Austin. She is a fan of classic rock, country and classical music but her favorite music is the sound of a good thunderstorm or a howling blizzard. Two of her favorite past times are baking artisan breads for her friends and spending quality time with her two German Shepherds.</span>
